What's more, the extra points are breakfast until 10:30, which is more suitable for guests who cannot get up early. What I lose more points is that the red dragon fruit is on the first day of breakfast, but there is no more in the next few days. Another time, the beef vermicelli soup had no beef. In addition, the white porridge but no fermented bean curd and salted duck eggs is also disappointing. Coffee beans are also not satisfactory.

In general, the price/performance ratio is very high. The location and traffic are also good, and parking is free. Compared with the international luxury hotels, the software and services are not stable enough.
